   Set Result      = '澜己(4.0)'     
      ,NormalFlag  = '0'                   
      ,PanicFlag   = '0'                   
      ,DeltaFlag   = '0'                   
      ,TransFlag   = '1'                   
      ,ResultID    = '501'
      ,ResultDate  = '2020-11-24'
      ,ResultTime  = '16:15:34'
 Where SPECIMENNUM = '2011240228'  
   AND OrderCode   = '2015'    
   And LabCode     = '2015'   
   And TRANSFLAG   < '2'                   

Update SLA_LabMaster                       
   Set JStatus = '2'                       
 Where SPECIMENNUM  = '2011240228'  
   AND OrderCode    = '2015'    
   AND Receiptdate = '2020-11-24'    
   And JStatus < '3'
